1)
The Mindset of a Leader
This time representatives from various countries have come, and when they return, they must work hard. What do you think? Between the work done at the Washington conference and the work done in your hometown, which do you think was done with more enthusiasm? Let’s see a show of hands from those who think the activities during this time were more enthusiastic than those at the Washington conference. I see. That means until now, you all haven’t been working hard. (Laughter) 
Now, if you work harder than during the Washington conference, the level will change. Therefore, we must set the standard that what was done at the Washington conference is the minimum level. If we do that, we will develop. Since representatives from each country are working based on that standard, let’s find out about the people in each state of America. Here, state leaders, which was more enthusiastic, what you did during the Washington conference or what you did in your state? Let’s see a show of hands from state leaders within the U.S. Raise your hands if you were responsible in your state. Come over here, this way. If possible, come forward. (Brief commotion due to moving seats)
Now, let’s raise our hands once more. Put them down. I want to ask one thing, in your state on October 3, 1976, at the Belvedere training center.
* This speech was given during the meeting of American and world leaders, and the title was assigned by the editor.
8 The Mindset of a Leader
When you were active then and when you were active at the Washington conference, when did you work harder? “During the Washington conference.” Why is that? You should have done more…. You experienced how to work while participating this time, right? Now, you all should think the same way, just like international leaders when they return, considering what was done in Washington as the minimum standard, and set the principle that whether eating or sleeping, you must strive to go beyond that.
This will be a principle, a foundation that all members of the Unification Church around the world must now adopt as they move into a new era of higher dimensions. So, we must resolve that from now on, we will start in earnest based on that standard. If we look at it as the era of intention, it means entering a different dimension. Starting tomorrow, we will enter a different level.
Until now, in the era of your lives, you have been going up and down, up and down, in the restoration process. You could do it again if you couldn’t, but from now on, that will not be the case. We are entering an era where only the upward movement will occur.
Why is that? Because until now, we have not been able to surpass the line of corruption, on a global standard. As a result, the good spirits in the spirit world, which corresponds to the angelic world, could not fully support the religious believers on this earth, which corresponds to the Adamic world. Why? Because the people in the Adamic world have not surpassed the realm of corruption. However, due to the Washington conference in 1976, the good spirits in the spirit world can now cooperate with the earth.
Then, if we say it corresponds to the angelic world, what happens? Until now, your ancestors could receive the mission within the realm of angels, we can say. Just as angels cooperated in God's creation work, your ancestors can cooperate for the purpose of the re-creation of the completion of Adam.
What does that mean? It means that in our restoration providence, we can develop through the direct support of our ancestors from God, and at the same time, we enter a time when our ancestors, that is, the good angelic world, will fight and take responsibility against Satan. In other words, they will enter a time when they can defend against Satan and fight directly against him. Therefore, from now on, a unified phenomenon will unfold in the world, and we will enter a time when we can be mobilized under a single operational command on earth.
In the spirit world, there is no such thing as America or England. There is none. They do not recognize any of that. There are no nations there. The goal is one nation. And in what form is it? It is in the form of religion. There are many religious realms such as Buddhism, Christianity, and Islam. However, until now, they have all been divided into factions and could not make horizontal connections.
But now that the Washington conference has ended, it has become a time to establish an order that can weave this horizontally. Thus, as the spirit world takes on a unified organizational form, the earthly world will also take on a unified organizational form, and such a unified organizational form cannot be opposed by Satan, as it will yield no results. Ultimately, the positions of spiritual superiority and inferiority will be reversed. This is something you must understand.
You may think that it seems like just words, but do you really think so? “Yes.” Even if you don’t believe it, you must believe it. Believe it. The dimension will change. The world of Satan is gradually retreating, while the world of good spirits is gradually winning. It is changing. So, this is a time of changing dimensions.
Therefore, it is not like before, going up and down, but only upward movement will occur. So how much effort do you need to put in? You must do more than what was done at the Washington conference. If you do more than that, you will develop. There will only be upward movement. The activities at this Washington conference have become a standard in the spirit world. When you move beyond that, you will be ascending. You must understand that this has become a standard. This means that heaven is with you. 
10 The Mindset of a Leader
Heaven cooperated because…. Do you understand? “Yes.” Do you understand why it commands you to do the minimum and more? “Yes.”
That means you must not go down. You must not go down. If you move based on the standard of the activities of those who attended this conference, heaven will surely cooperate, and you will undoubtedly make progressive advancements. Why? Because the content in the spirit world is changing like this. Now you have understood this clearly.
You must launch a full-scale attack on the capitals of each country as evidence of the victory of the Washington conference.
So now, when you return, where will you work? Just like in Washington, you must mobilize the capitals of each country, the capital of your nation. Now, this means that you…. Just as I took responsibility here three and a half years ago and swore before heaven, you must now act directly towards the capital, not just locally. I send you with such a mission!
Three years ago, the teacher and you…. You are at a time to attack the capital, but the teacher has come up from the bottom to attack the capital. The dimensions and times are different. When you look at such responsible areas, you must understand that your starting point regarding your country carries a higher level of responsibility than when the teacher started in America.
Therefore, you must take all those weapons, whether they are made into films or any materials. When you see that we placed advertisements for the Washington conference in three newspapers for four pages over two days, you can understand how fierce the battle in Washington was. This will become a treasure of our church throughout history.
Even if they say that Washington was all done in a big way, the people of your country cannot deny it when they see the film and watch the movie. Also, although the Washington Post and the New York Times opposed us, since all the citizens were connected, they could not hit us or oppose us, so even conditional newspapers recording the coverage came out. Why was that? Because the citizens all returned, it became a big deal.
When you look at what was published in the newspaper on the 18th, comparing the funeral of Mao Zedong with the incident of Rev. Moon in Washington, you can see how different the dimensions were. The Washington Post clearly testified to that. That is all evidence material. Also, that day, September 18, is the day when Mao Zedong, who is said to be the number one in Asia, passed away, and the day when Rev. Moon, who is said to be the number one religious leader in Asia, ascended. It is a historic day.
People in the East also think that way. As an Easterner, they believe that Rev. Moon is the best. So, we must focus on all such promotional materials and launch a full-scale attack in broad daylight. Now, you will go into your country and spread from the city center to every village. It is a full-scale attack. We will take an offensive nationwide.
Next, we must make all the houses we bought into photographs. This is what we have done over the past three years. And the book titled 'Day of Hope' will come out in two volumes, which exceeds one thousand pages; all of this is what we have done in a year. Now, from Yankee Stadium to the Washington conference, that will also be about two thousand pages. When you lay this out, you will see that in three and a half years, this person has done such and such things. Think about it.
Now you have entered a good era where you can attack the capital of your country…. If in these three and a half years you can push through your country, then as I mentioned earlier, holding a conference in Moscow will not be a problem. If you do not do this in a short time, it will become an empty theory. What was said this morning will become an empty theory.
Now, do you understand that you are bringing a good gift? “Yes.” When you see that, you will go “Oh!” It is said that this was done not in welcome but in the midst of strong opposition, and it can be believed that “if it had been welcomed, it would have completely ruined America.” If they had supported it, America would have completely turned around. Therefore, now we can show that Rev. Moon of the Unification Church has such influence and that the Unification Church has such power.
We must start moving from the highest leaders of the nation and state with the materials of victory.
So now, you must go back and meet the president, the prime minister, and the members of parliament and say, “Push me. Let’s see if I can do it or not. Let’s see if I can save this country or not.” You must have that kind of bold play. You must move the highest leaders of the nation like that.
Then you must prepare to say, “In order to open a new path for our country to be revived, we need to bring thousands of international mobile units gathered from around the world into our country. Will you, president, prime minister, and citizens, unite and welcome them? If you will welcome them, I will bring them.” You must prepare for this. Now, gather a thousand, about three thousand people, and make a big noise. That is what we are going to do. We are going to do that. Therefore, you must prepare for this as soon as possible. Think about facing the prime minister and the highest leaders of the country. Do you understand? “Yes.”
Then state leaders, you are all…. Your state is your nation. The states of America are one nation. You must think of the states of America as one nation. Therefore, you must discuss with the state governors. If you do not, the state will not survive; if you do not discuss with all the state legislators who lead the state, the state will not survive. Have that confidence. When we have the state general elections this time, we can create such explosive movements. We will bring materials to the state.
Moreover, there is no one in America who does not know Rev. Moon, right? Those who do not know are fine. If the world has made such a fuss and you did not know, does that make you a person? What good is it to live in America? It is only a burden. It is useless. It is a parasite that only causes harm. Everyone knows. When you say “Rev. Moon,” whether good or bad, they will go “Ah!” They cannot help but be interested. (Laughter) The reaction is overwhelmingly large. If they did not know, they would say, “Wow, I didn’t know that.”
Yano! Matsuda! Have you come? You haven’t. How long will it take to make the film? You need to make it quickly. I told you to make it within two weeks, but it needs to be done faster than the Yankee Stadium conference. You must understand how expensive this film is. You must understand how terrifying a weapon it is in the restoration providence. It is a terrifying weapon.
People like Billy Graham took 25 or 30 years to achieve something, but the teacher did it in three and a half years, three and a half years. And while Billy Graham did it within America, I came to America as a Korean, facing opposition and having interpreters. That is why I have materials that no one can challenge, no matter what kind of propaganda I do.
And among the current state leaders, there are many white people. There are many real Americans. So, if you say, “Don’t say this. This time at the Washington conference, people of color came out and supported Rev. Moon, so if this continues, it will be a big problem for white people. Do you think you will be able to be governors in the future?” If you talk about these issues, it will be accepted. And to unite people of color, you must put me forward. You cannot do it, but I can. This gives you a chance to make friends in this regard. And when it comes to elections, you need people, right? You need votes, right? The outcome will depend on who absorbs the most votes from people of color, and I will cooperate then, so let’s unite. So when you return, who will you show the movie to first? To the governor, starting with the governor, you will show it to the key officials of the state. Then you will show it to all the upper and lower house members of that state. That is how it must be done. Then, since we have held a conference for scientists, we will also need to reach out to scholars and universities.
There are scholars who are all related to us. All the scholars who will come next have the mindset of a leader. We should go find those scholars, gather the professors from that school, and have them sign under the name of a certain professor, saying, "On a certain day, I will show a photo of Reverend Moon. If you want to judge Reverend Moon after seeing the photo, come." This is how we will invite everyone and show them. After that, we will also show it to the students of the school. Do you understand? "Yes." You should also have the mindset of the president of that country, the prime minister, and those in high positions...

The issue of whether your work will yield results in that state in the future will depend on who can play that game quickly, and whether the leaders of the country will return to the will of heaven quickly or not will also be determined. That's what I think. As a leader of the organization that Reverend Moon guides, you must confidently and passionately speak to the whole group about that powerful background.

I am not afraid of anything. I have met everyone from senators to the president since coming to America, and I have met everyone I needed to meet. How wonderful it would have been if I had had this material back then, if I could have shown a movie! At that time, I only had a palm and passing guests. There were only faces of Eastern people. The signboards were the faces. (Laughter) Even with that, I did it, so if you can't do it, it doesn't make sense. Why can't you do it with the same face? Why can't you do it as the same people?

Have the determination to move the highest responsible person. Now, even if you make friends with the authority of heaven, think about making friends with high-ranking friends, and even when you have dinner, think about eating with high-ranking friends. Don't do it trivially. Do you understand? "Yes." So, even if you are a small female leader, you should bring rice cakes and confront the president. "I thought you had a big disposition, but what is this?" and list unbelievable things in a cunning manner. "If you, as president, can't believe that, this country will not be able to lead the world in the future." This is how you confront them.

And do not think, "Ah! Our Teacher Moon is like Buddha, Confucius, or Jesus." You should think of swallowing all of that. You should think of swallowing Christianity and everything else. That's what I mean. The countries and religious nations they established have all been consumed by communism, and we cannot let that happen. You should also have that disposition now. The reason I say to have that disposition is to give you that authority. Can you do that? "Yes."

When you kick a ball, you should kick it beautifully from the center to break through to the heavens... You need to have that mindset. So, are you confident? "Yes." Therefore, you should become famous, and the president should think, "Oh, if that woman hadn't married, how great it would have been to have her as my wife!" and you should make it so that he cannot help but write to you and cannot help but follow you.

If there is someone like that, you can say, "I will introduce you to a woman from the Unification Church who is more excellent than I am." (Laughter) "There is a woman who is better looking than I am, taller than I am, and has more guts than I do, so what do you think?" and he will open his mouth and say, "Ah!" (Laughter) Why are you laughing? You should have the thought of marrying off the president. All of this is done by people, by people.

Therefore, in the future, you need to lay the groundwork to play such games with the responsible leaders of that state and with the leaders of the country. Laying that groundwork was my dream, and now I see we are entering an era where we can do that. If you run for about three years like this, what do you think will happen? People will say, "Let's see what will happen to that person who came here three years ago with nothing but empty hands. Let's see what he does. He was making a lot of noise; let's see what he does."

When I met the American senators and said, "I will gather many young people and support you for about two years..." no one believed it. Nowadays, they will believe it. (Laughter) Now they believe it. Therefore, you should learn from the methods I used over the past three years. Create a mobilization team and start problems from the bottom to rise up. Go all the way to the top and make a big noise! Do you understand? "Yes." Now, go out and do it just as I strategized. Can you do that? "Yes." Can women do it? "Yes." You need to answer. You should always be first, not second. You should answer when I ask. Now, do you understand? "Yes."

Make bigger plans than the Washington Conference and act vigorously. So, over the past two weeks, I wanted to know how... After the vigorous operation during the Washington Conference, I wanted to know if what you did over the past two weeks was better or worse than the Washington Conference operation. Was it more vigorous or less vigorous? Answer me. "It was not." Why are you laughing? You should open your eyes wide and say, "I worked hard." Be honest. Was it more vigorous? "Yes."

What does Neil (the president of the American Unification Church) think? "Are you asking in comparison to the Washington operation or in comparison to before that?" In comparison to the Washington operation. "I think it was more vigorous than during the Washington Conference. However, it was not as vigorous as on the last day of the Washington Conference. This is my honest answer." Then, from now on, there will be no problem exceeding that, right? "Yes." Since everyone moved, now with that confidence and experience, if you take action, you will surely do better, right? Did you do it two by two? So, you couldn't do that and are this comfortable? Can you eat? You received the Teacher's special command, and you can't do that and still sleep? Sleep?

When you came here today to meet the Teacher, did you have the feeling that you couldn't lift your face like a sinner? I think heaven had a cooperative system ready as soon as the Teacher spoke, but it didn't work out because you didn't reach that point. If you had thought of it as a matter of life and death and cried, clung on, and fought harder than any fight, there would have been a way.

What do you think? The thought of "Ah, I can't do any more than this" is your own thought. Up to now, what has moved is what you have moved. You can't do it with that. "If each of you doesn't witness to two people during these two weeks, the world will perish, and heaven and earth will perish. It will really perish." Did you feel that? Have you made the determination, "I will take responsibility for that person with my neck on the line"? Have you taken it seriously? I think you haven't.

I believe that if each person could witness to two people in one week, it would surely... If everyone set that principle and pushed forward, I would have been able to do everything I wanted to do in these two years, and I would have been able to fulfill everything God wanted. I believe that if everyone had decided, "After this conference, I will definitely harvest a few people before heaven," such things would have been possible.

Now, as you return, set a plan with your members that says, "A few months later, I will do this." Swear that "We will do this," and make a resolution that you will take responsibility for this work, and you will do it, and I will do it. If the group is small, each of you should make such a plan centered around yourselves and swear to it. You must do that. So, now, I must return with the determination to be the experimental one who can implement what I couldn't do, witnessing to one person a week or two people every two weeks, and establish my face before heaven.

Why must it be done that way? Why must it be done that way? If we do not set any limits by 1978, the heavenly operation, the Teacher's operation regarding this world will completely collapse. It will completely collapse. This must match these two worlds... If this is long, it's good, but if it's short, it will crash down heavily. Heaven's plan waits, but this will crash down heavily. You must understand that.

You must emphasize that such members must also become those who can break through that week. If you can do that, you will have more than enough during these two years. You will have more than enough.

Have the confidence and belief that you will become the ultimate victor. Now, even when you pray, you must know how to command, "If there are good ancestors among my ancestors, listen. If you do not cooperate with me, you will fall under the laws of the spirit world, and if you do cooperate with me, you will enjoy the benefits of this era and the privileges of entering the heavenly kingdom, so all spirits of the spirit world, mobilize." 

Then, the ancestral spirits who hear your words will all coordinate behind the scenes and will teach you in your dreams while you sleep, and when you pray, they will surely guide you with revelations and will work to bind us together. You must command it to be so.

Therefore, even if the unchanging spirit world is mobilized, you must say, "If I mobilize the spirit world and then fail, that will rather block my path, so from now on, I will only advance with an unwavering attitude." There can be no retreat. If there is a retreat, you will be caught. That is why you must rise. When facing spirits, you must say, "Cooperate with me and rest assured. I will go this way." You must set that determination. So, "All my ancestors and all my distant relatives, cooperate with me." If you can push forward with such a background that supports you, the whole will cooperate. You must feel that.

Whenever you wish for the inspiration of the spirit world, if you suddenly feel like going somewhere, you must run there immediately. Do not stop that. If you want to say something to someone, say it right then and start doing such things from now on. And you should now have the pride that you are the one in that state who sleeps the least, who puts in more effort for heaven than anyone else, and who loves and cares for that state more than anyone else. You should have the pride that you have the conditions to be able to do that.

Therefore, if you have become the responsible person of that state, you must make sure that there is no valley or place in that state that you have not visited. You must go everywhere until your feet wear out. And say, "As I move like this, you spirits of the spirit world, if there are any useful people, give them a conscientious stimulus. I will come back again." Then you will look back a second time.

I think if you do that more than three times, problems will arise. Therefore, when you go once, meet one person at that house, when you go a second time, meet another person, and when you go a third time, meet three people at one house and speak to them, if they do not listen to that, that house will perish. All the blessings of that house will be transferred. The spirit world will attack. What does that mean? Because they did not treat guests well, they did not give proper treatment to the distinguished guests of the heavenly kingdom, they will pay for that. This is a dream-like story. It is a dream-like story, but you must understand that it is a reality. The Teacher is a dream-like person. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do not be the person who, after failing despite the cooperation of the spirit world, says, "Oh, I wish the spirit world had not helped me." Be the person who says, "Wow, I'm glad they supported me. That makes sense."

So, while saying, "Wind, blow! Typhoon, come! All persecution, come! The more you come, the richer I become. I will become the ultimate victor of this country." You must have that confidence. "Look at me over three years, look at me over ten years. If I do not die and go out, I will have plenty of money, power, and everything." You must have that confidence, like the Teacher.

Am I rich now in America? Even if I make you all work like servants, even after doing all the work, I am still here. (Laughter) That's right, isn't it? "Yes." It is the same for you as you go. It is the same for you as you go. Just as if you plant a willow tree, a willow will grow, if you have become a branch of Reverend Moon, you should become like Reverend Moon. It is the same. Can you do that? "Yes." Have that disposition. Have that belief. If this belief is weak, do not eat. "Ah, this is a more certain truth than being hungry." When you are hungry, do you long for food? Can you do that? "Yes." Then surely you will all become successful. Do you know why? Because it is important, I am saying this.

Now, you must know that it is becoming such a time. If you do not understand, believe it. After tomorrow, the Teacher's prayers will change. They will be different from the prayers until now.

Now, in front of the communist world, we must resolve all the grievances of those who died at the hands of Lenin, Stalin, and Mao Zedong, so that we can mobilize those spirits and send them to the communist world. That is why we pray like that. It will change. After that, all the dead spirits who opposed Christianity and good people will come back to make up for the games they played on earth. The Christians who prayed to subjugate and overthrow the Roman Empire while being persecuted and massacred for 400 years will now be pushed into the country of evil, the communist world.

And this year, many Unification Church people, especially leaders, have gone to the spirit world. What kind of disease did they die from the most? Cancer and chronic diseases. Isn't that strange? But it is not strange. I think they went to carry those chronic diseases to make up for them rather than die.

So, they will pray for the Teacher in the Unification Church and try to resolve the resentment of those who died without fulfilling the will. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Then it will be really good.
"Yes." In order to do that, you must not fall under the conditions for indemnity. We must not fall under the conditions for indemnity. Now, when mobilizing the spirit world and activating it, if you cannot take responsibility, you must understand that you and your direct descendants will receive indemnity. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." It will definitely happen. You need to be aware of that.

During the time of Jesus, miracles were performed, but there were no disciples capable of supporting that, leading to the downfall of his clan and the nation of Israel, and all the closest people went to hell. It is the same principle. Did Israel not perish because Jesus was killed? It is the same. On the day you take full responsibility, if you are struck, everything will be taken away.

This kind of historical narrative is being shared for the first time today, right here, in front of you. You need to understand how fearful this place is. You might think, "I don't know what that is," but go to the spirit world. Go to the spirit world. You will understand how true the teacher's words are at that time.

Because the spirits that were massacred by them in the real world will massacre them all. They all died miserably. That is the mindset of the leaders. If that does not happen, then God is a dead God. The conclusion is that God has no senses and no bones. "Yes." Good. That means it is not just between me and you, but between God and you. That will become your eternal vow. I will trust you.

A nation with the economic power to move the world must emerge. 

Now that you generally understand, we need to make work plans. Would it be good if we became the richest in the world? Do we need money? "Yes." Would it be better if we had more money than the United States? "Yes." Would it be good if the Unification Church had all the best young people in the world? "Yes." Therefore, we must gather the world's wealth and become the richest, and the Unification Church must have more of the world's best young people than any other nation. This is the teacher's goal.

In the future world, it will depend on who controls the money... You need to understand this. The current era is one where the development of productive goods and scientific civilization has brought forth convenient products for humanity, meaning that the countries capable of producing these goods possess the world's wealth. Such countries are advanced nations. For those countries, the market is everywhere. The entire world is a market. Therefore, it is impossible not to become rich. Thus, having productive power is the highest goal of a nation, and each country has competed based on that. What was once one advanced nation has now become a group of advanced nations.

However, what problem arises here? No matter how much productive power a country has, if it cannot secure the market rights to sell, that country becomes a secondary nation. The era of struggle for productive power has passed. That was what dominated the world. Now, that era is passing, and what is needed is to win in the battle for market control to possess the economic power of the world.

The Age of Judgment and Us
Everyone, when we talk about judgment, a courtroom comes to mind. When you go to that courtroom, there is a judge, a prosecutor, a defense attorney, a prisoner, and an audience of non-prisoners, good people. Why is there judgment? Because the law has been broken. In other words, as a result of breaking the law, sin arises... When one breaks the law and gets caught in conditions, we know that one must pay the corresponding penalty.

To become a true person, one must unite with true law, true words.
If it is a country, there is a law that defends the sovereignty centered on that country, and that law is the word and truth that can establish the sovereignty of that country. If you live according to that law, if you become the person that the law desires, you will not be caught by the law. What must you become as a person who is not caught by the law? What is the purpose of establishing the law? It is to become one with the sovereign. So what is to be done? It is to advance to a better place. This is the content and purpose of establishing the law. This is the same for one nation, the same for society, the same for our Unification Church organization, and the same for families. Following such principles, our social situation hopes to develop towards one purpose.

People with such thoughts are now opposing the Unification Church. Can such a thing happen? They are saying shocking things, claiming that God’s most shocking sorrow became the motive for salvation. The moment Jesus was dying on the cross was an astonishing scene for God. When Jesus died, God had no choice but to be in a position of not knowing. That’s why Jesus said, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani (My God, my God, why have you forsaken me)?” He asked why he was forsaken. But what does forsaking mean? Jesus should not have died at that time.

Now we must raise this again and let people know that God has been alive in the historical process. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Through this history of struggle, Christianity has laid the foundation for the spiritual world. We must complete the fundamental restoration of Adam and Eve centered on spirit and body. From a spiritual perspective, Jesus is the husband, and the Holy Spirit is the wife. Believing and coming out based on this foundation of spiritual parents is what Christianity is now. Therefore, Christianity must abandon the world. Only spiritually... How about the Unification Church? The Unification Church is different. It is a new Christianity. So, did you believe in Jesus well? "Yes." Then why did you come to the Unification Church instead of just believing in Jesus? The Unification Church is not a church of Jesus. Now, even if I die, know that God's will will conquer this world and more. I will go to the heavenly kingdom as a victorious son, not as a failure like Jesus.

So, since today is Children’s Day, let us bring the glory of children... The Harmony of Science and the Quest for Absolute Values
Respected Chairperson, distinguished scientists, professors, and scholars! I sincerely welcome all of you who are attending the 5th International Conference on Unified Science today. I am especially pleased to see those of you who have attended this conference repeatedly.

You have been discussing the issue of "absolute values" for many years, and this year you have gathered under the theme of "The Quest for Absolute Values."

To find absolute values, we must clarify the origin of the existence of humans and all things in the universe. The question arises whether the origin of the universe is from the existence (유) or from non-existence (무), but as you well know, both natural sciences and social sciences, philosophy, and religion do not explore the truth in the world of non-existence but seek to find some causal existence in the world of existence, and from there, seek the principles of existence and operation of all things, including humans. Ultimately, it is about clarifying the content of existence and establishing the reasons and values of all existence by creating relationships between existents.

If the minimum unit necessary for the formation of matter is an element, it is defined as existence (유), and the foundation of element formation cannot be non-existence (무) but must logically start from absolute existence (절대유). Modern science sees that even the minimum unit of matter, the atom, exists due to some fundamental force, leading to the conclusion that this force also originates from existence (유). Considering the vast universe magnified from the smallest point, and from the perspective that results arise from causes, we can understand that we humans are ultimately not causal existences but result existences, and thus there must be a causal existence. Correcting the illogicality of some scholars who claim that existence (유) arises from non-existence (무) and establishing a logical system that states that absolute existence (절대유) generates and develops into small existence (소유) and large existence (대유) is fundamentally scientific, as it connects the causes of all things and allows them to act organically.

From this perspective, the traditional theory of evolution must be re-examined. For evolution to occur, there must be action, and for action to occur, it must be through force. Therefore, can action give rise to a greater force? It is absolutely impossible for action to create a greater existence, as force is consumed through action. The principle is that force is consumed through action, and the question is whether it can evolve rather than degenerate, and whether it can have a directional tendency to develop into something more valuable and higher-dimensional.

The development of the universe due to corresponding and opposing actions
While it may seem like evolution at first glance, the explanation of mutations as described by De Vries in the stepwise creation process of the universe does not hold. For something to become more valuable and progressive, a third force must be applied; therefore, if all animals are not continuing to evolve today and if evolution has stopped in humans, it indicates that the ultimate purpose of the first causal existence that made humans a result must have been clearly directed toward humans. Here, we can first establish the logic that "the first causal existence existed beforehand."

Next, the question arises whether existence comes first in this universe or whether force comes first. No existence can survive and act without some force. There is a force that enables action within each individual existence and between existences. The question then becomes how this force arises.

For force to arise, there must be some subject and object beforehand; it cannot arise without them. In other words, the relationship between subject and object is a precondition. For example, even in an atom, there is a subject, the proton, and an object, the electron, which together enable action. Since the action of force begins with the purpose of unifying the subject and object, when we ask whether force comes first or the subject and object come first, it is undoubtedly the case that the subject and object come first, and the action of force is a process phenomenon aimed at the unification of the subject and object.

Because the action of force varies depending on the differences and weights of the subject-object relationship, whenever various forces act, their directionality and purpose will inevitably differ, leading to a diverse world of existences. Thus, the action of force between any subject and object also acts with directionality and purpose because the fundamental subject and object among the first causal existences act with directionality and purpose.

Now, an existence in which the subject and object are completely unified within the individual takes a subjective or objective position to establish a relationship with another existence, thereby developing into a being with greater directionality and purpose. The action of the subjective existence and the objective existence always develops into a greater existence through mutual exchange for some common benefit.

This vast universe is a joint purpose of subject and object, so it possesses a cosmic force that protects itself, while at the same time, it nurtures and protects those existences that are completely unified as subjects and objects. On the other hand, when there are existences that have not unified as subjects and objects and that infringe upon those that have, it acts to reject them. This is why the permanence of existence is possible. The force that assists in this is called corresponding action (상응작용), while the opposing force can be called opposing action (상극작용). It can also be referred to as action and reaction.

This applies to both the material world and the human world. When our mind and body are united, we feel joy because we are under the protection of the cosmic force that assists us. However, when the mind and body are not united, we feel pain and react against it. The pain caused by illness is the same. When the subjective elements and relative elements within the body are not harmoniously unified, we lose cosmic protective power, and as a result of that reaction, we feel pain, which is a great suffering. At this time, the medication prescribed by a doctor is aimed at quickly opening the way for the subject and object to harmoniously unify. This applies to individuals as well as families.

For example, before marriage, men may like other men and women may like other women, but after marriage, no one welcomes interference between the two. The family after marriage is where the subject and object are completely unified, and they feel happiness and satisfaction under the protection of cosmic power. However, if a second woman or a second man intervenes, there is a risk that the force that unites the couple will be destroyed, which leads to a reaction against it. This reaction is not necessarily bad; rather, it serves as a stimulus that encourages them to quickly go and unite with their subject or object to receive the protection of cosmic power and achieve permanence. In other words, it becomes a force that promotes completion.

Electrical action also works smoothly when the subject, the positive, and the object, the negative, unite, but positive repels positive and negative repels negative. Whenever any existence forms a relationship by finding a subject and object, the same law applies...
It is through this that one feels stability and joy.  
All beings reproduce in likeness to the First Cause.  
According to the logic described above, when a subject and an object become one through interaction, they enter into the cosmic realm of protection. Since every action we observe in the universe is a resultant action derived from the First Causal Being, it is a natural theory that there exists a causal entity at the center of it all. Just as children resemble their parents, the results resemble their causes, allowing us to identify the causal existence by observing all things.  
When we look at the seeds of all plants, we see that they contain two relative halves that, while being a complete unity, interact through the embryo within a single shell to reproduce life. Even when we look at an egg, there is an embryo between the yolk and the egg white, all enclosed within a single shell, forming a unity. The same applies to human embryos.  
All living beings, whether human or plant, reproduce in likeness to their causes when the subject and object become one through interaction, ultimately returning to the fundamental source. If all of this resembles the ultimate First Cause, then that First Causal Being must possess a subject-like quality as a fundamental form of complete unity with all existence.  
The Purpose of the Gradual Creation of the Universe  
So, what is the purpose of this gradual creation of all things in the universe? It is seen as having begun for the existence of human beings. In other words, humans can be regarded as the fruit and miniature model of all existence, embodying all elements of minerals, plants, and animals, making them the highest form of existence.  
However, since humans are ultimately resultant beings, it follows that there exists a First Causal Being from which they have emerged in likeness. That is, there must be an absolute subject that pertains to humanity, and since we are personal beings, that subject must also undoubtedly be a personal being. This First Causal Absolute is referred to as existence in philosophy and as God in religion.  
Today, due to theories such as evolution, material dialectics, epistemology, idealism, and materialism, the realm of thought in the world has fallen into contradictions and confusion, necessitating a re-examination to establish absolute truth, which is essential for the formation of an absolute value world. An absolute value existence is eternal, unchanging, and unique. Thus, what is the principle of eternity, unchangeability, and absoluteness in the universe? It concludes with the relationship between cause and effect, subject and object.  
Applying this to human society, the core lies in the relationships of parent and child and husband and wife. One is a vertical relationship of subject and object, while the other is a horizontal relationship of subject and object. Both exist in a higher dimensional relationship of subject and object, where the vertical union becomes a new subject and the horizontal union becomes a new object, entering a state of harmonious interaction, forming a unified, three-dimensional movement centered on love, which is the model of the ideal family, the basic unit of human society. In this sense, love must be recognized as the most valuable thing.  
The ultimate source of love does not begin with us humans but starts from the absolute unchanging causal subject. Therefore, the family centered on this love becomes the fundamental unit for the ideal realization of human society. From here, the ideal world of absolute value, where the love-filled unified realm expands into nations and the world, promising eternal happiness of absolute value, will surely come.  
I hope that this conference will greatly contribute to solving the various problems facing humanity today, correcting the future course, and achieving the common goal of "the pursuit of absolute value" through harmonious cooperation in academia, thereby constructing an ideal world of peace, happiness, and love for humanity. Thank you.  
Reflection  
All people who constitute the Unification Church, whether they are Koreans, Japanese, or from Western societies, in other words, all races have been mobilized and have been related to this until now.  
Reflecting on the past 36 years, I feel that the path of the will is difficult.  
Looking back now, sometimes, ten or twenty years ago, when I reflect on what remained in the teacher's mind, I realize that many different people came into contact with the teacher during the journey and then fell away, while a considerable number of those who reconnected were not only aware of Heaven's will but also received direct guidance from Heaven, swearing countless oaths and making numerous efforts, and these people come to mind now.  
The 36 years spent in this way is a long time if considered long, and a short time if considered short. Historically, it is a brief period, yet it is filled with unforgettable events, unforgettable people, and unforgettable human relationships, reminding me once again that the path of the will is truly difficult.  
When I think about this, what comes to mind now? When people who thought that they could not do without this will fall away, they do so thinking that there might be something new outside of this will. Most of those people left in pursuit of their dreams, believing they could realize them externally, but they find that they have not achieved those dreams.  
Among those people, there are young men and women who have betrayed the will in search of romantic relationships, and there are those who have done so to attend school or for their own success, and there are various types. Among them are older individuals, middle-aged individuals, and young individuals, and many of them now deeply regret their choices. They cannot forget the past and are filled with regret.  
Among them, there are even more miserable types of people, and I think we should reflect on this under the title of "Reflection." What kind of people are they?  
Those who have become the focus of everyone's attention, who remain in people's memories, and who have received praise from others saying, "I want to be like that person," are those who have stood in significant positions within the Unification Church, and they are miserable. They valued the will above all else and regarded it as the highest, sacrificing everything without hesitation. They abandoned everything without regret and were in a position where they felt happiness by sacrificing everything for that one will. When they turn back and face the world, they encounter the very things they had abandoned, and they cannot recover the feelings they had before they abandoned them.  
What do such people say? They thought there would be joy outside the Unification Church, and they believed there would be some hope for themselves, but the more they go out, the more despair they find. When they turn away and face the world, they find that what they hoped for is not greater than what they abandoned, and their thoughts grow stronger: "It was because of you that I abandoned the will." However, even if they have abandoned the will, they cannot completely sever ties with it. When they experience unspeakable pain and loneliness, they cannot help but struggle.  
Four Types of People Following the Will  
From such a perspective, how much do those who used to see the path of the will as ordinary long for it? You may not feel this. You are going through this now. There is such a difference. Those who are in such positions may find it difficult now, but no matter how difficult or miserable it is, they think, "How wonderful it would have been if I had continued to be there!" and their longing is incomparable to their current struggles.  
Thus, those who have fallen away from the path of the will gather together. The church keeps its doors open, inviting those who want to return. The teacher does not reprimand them when they come back, saying, "Oh, you have come back." Instead, he treats them naturally. However, they carry an indescribable shame or a sense of self-reproach and regret.  
Their thoughts, "The whole family must see me this way," confine them. They think, "The teacher must see me this way," and that thought confines them entirely. Even when treated sincerely, they do not feel that sincerity. No matter how much they are comforted, those words are temporary. They see the comfort as being given with the thought, "You are such a person." Even if they come back and do something for the will, people see them as someone who will fall away again. As time passes, with the emergence of 36 families and the lineage of blessed families, and as they age into their 20s and 30s, the Unification Church develops and lays a foundation, they see that it unfolds beyond their imagined ideals.  
When we think of such a past, we must recognize that we are in a position where we can leave such a past today. Because they encounter such environments, some say, "Rather than living in Korea or Japan, if there is a Unification Church abroad, I should believe there." However, it is not that America is different or Europe is different; the Unification Church is all under the teacher's guidance. Nowadays, Koreans are interacting and becoming a global church.  
When we see this, those who have believed in the Unification Church will feel that there is no place to find solace in their hearts, no matter where they go on Earth. This will also be true in the spirit world. The reason I am sharing this with you is that we must understand how much a single mistake in our lives can have a fatal impact. It is extremely difficult to escape from that environment.  
When you go to a place like prison, you can feel such things vividly. A person who intended to live rightly may end up in prison due to a chance encounter with the wrong friend or through some mistake. When one must live their whole life in prison, what thoughts occupy their mind? Whenever they have time, they think, "If only I hadn't done that back then, I would have achieved my dreams." It is very difficult to escape from that state. They think, "If I hadn't done this, I would have surely become a good person." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." We must recognize that such people exist. They are miserable people.  
Next, there are those who have been with the Unification Church for a long time, those who remain. They say they are following the path of the will, but what have they done over the past 10 or 20 years? The principles have presented that "the path to take is this way, this way," but there are those who have not practiced any of it and just followed along.  
What kind of people are they? The more they think about the past, the more they feel ashamed, especially as the years go by. They have become accustomed to just going back and forth, attending on Sundays without making any progress, merely existing in a state of stagnation. Because they have no experience of actively practicing for the will, they are indifferent to whether others think it is good or bad. After spending 10 years like this, they finally realize, "I am in such a position," and they feel ashamed.  
Then, what kind of people are there? There are those who stand at the forefront of the will and strive to do even more. Among people, there are those who boast about the achievements they have made while leading, and there are also those who feel that they still have a long way to go and feel ashamed of what they have done in the past, feeling embarrassed about what the will demands of them.  
When we consider these types of people, who will ultimately stand at the last front? Those who are willing to sacrifice their entire lives, realizing their shortcomings and feeling compelled to do more, are the ones who ultimately remain until the end.  
In this view, when we look at those who have betrayed the will and left, those who are in an intermediate position, those who have not yet separated from the world and are merely going back and forth like the world, those who, from the standpoint of the will, want to boast about even a little they have done, and those who, from a willful standpoint, do not examine themselves but feel their shortcomings even while sacrificing themselves, the ones who remain are the last type.  
What kind of person is this last type? What kind of thoughts does this type of person have? They understand what the path of restoration is. They think about how to walk the path of restoration. The path of restoration must go beyond the individual, beyond the family, beyond the tribe, beyond the nation, beyond the world, and ultimately reach before God. Therefore, they are those who feel compelled to strive harder as they progress.  
So, among such people, how can someone from Korea, for instance, transcend to a global level? They must think symbolically or concretely, saying, "The suffering I endure is not just for the Korean people, but I am suffering on behalf of all humanity." Such individuals put in a lot of effort.  
When we view this, it is the same today. Even among you, there are various thoughts and actions regarding the path of the will. Such phenomena will continue from now on. When we think about this, you must decide what kind of person you want to be. You must make this decision. You are currently in a position where you have not departed from this will, but in your heart, you have done various things. You may have come and gone in your heart, but if your body is still not in that position, you must realize that you are destined to make new decisions and move forward.  
One cannot boast of oneself without feeling the seriousness of the providence of restoration.  
Looking at your current state… In 1976, reflecting on our activities in the United States, from the Yankee Stadium event to the Washington event, we fought fiercely. This time, we have completed the scientists' conference. When I think about this experience, I feel that although I have said I would do it, it does not seem like there have been significant results.  
So, do you feel that the victory at the Washington event was absolutely necessary? "Yes." It is not easy to genuinely feel that it was a once-in-a-lifetime chance. More than anyone else…
People who are not risking their lives in that competition cannot feel it that way. Do you understand that? "Yes." If this fails, what happens? If this does not succeed, how much impact will it have, how much will it be fatal to oneself, and how much will it go against the providence of God? Have you realized that? "Yes." Well, you say "yes," but the degree of understanding is all different. (Laughter) If there are hundreds of people here, there are hundreds of levels of understanding.

When you look at it that way, if you know that this is a serious struggle that involves the universe, and if you fight with all your heart knowing what the consequences will be if you fail, then that is something to be proud of. So if you win, that is God's victory, as well as the victory of the Teacher, and undoubtedly my victory. That is a serious matter.

Can you stand before God and say, "I am a warrior who attended the Washington Conference. You need to recognize me"? "Yes." (Laughter) If God looks at the Washington Conference, it has historical significance, just as the Teacher said. But if there is a problem that causes a setback, how serious would it be for God to have to overcome this hurdle in the providence of restoration that has been going on for hundreds of thousands of years? The day you cross that boundary you longed to cross, the world changes.

There will be such moments, there must be such moments. If that moment were the Washington Conference, how serious would God have been? This is serious. And from the Teacher's perspective, when the Teacher knows God's will and risks his life to cross this ridge, how fearful and daunting that place must be. It must be so. Right? It must be. "Yes." If it is serious, then the Teacher must have been more serious than you. And God must have been more serious than the Teacher. From that standpoint, you are not as serious as God. You are not as serious as the Teacher.

When this result comes about, what do you have to boast about? Who do you want to boast to? Do you want to boast to your friends? Do you want to boast to your parents? Do you want to boast to the king of your country? Can you boast about that? God is standing in such a serious position, and can you not feel that seriousness and boast? Can you boast before the Teacher when you are not even as serious as the Teacher? "No." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Why am I saying this? What is your attitude like now after the Washington Conference? Are you trying to clash more, or are you just sitting there? (Mimicking. Laughter) Therefore, you need to understand that 1976 is both the most precious year and the most fearful year for our Unification Church. Now we are slowly crossing over this ridge. Do you want to go down like this? (Drawing on the board) "No." Then how do you want to go down? You have to go down. Which is better? Is this better, or is this better? (Pointing to the board) What will you do about that? This is a big problem. If you cross over and just go around in circles... there are all kinds of people.

Heaven takes by force
When you come in the morning and look around, many people are dozing off. It has become the beginning of December, and they are just dozing off without thinking about what has happened. If you are sleepy, don’t come here. Why are you coming? How disrespectful is that in front of the Teacher? How disrespectful is that in front of God? If you know that God is here and what kind of place this is, can you doze off? This time may be the only time in your life to meet God. Isn’t that right? You might miss the beloved person you have been searching for a thousand years because you dozed off.

Among those who are attending here, there are people who know that this time is serious and are paying attention, and then there are those who think, "Oh, I just came because the Teacher talks annually. I’m just listening with my ears and looking with my eyes." And then there are those who say, "Well, I came because I was told to come. I don’t feel responsible," and just doze off.

You are the same. People can make mistakes, and everyone’s path can be bent. There cannot always be only good things. This is always the case. After good things happen, there will always come a dangerous time when that individual either stays or falls.

When you think about the members in the New York area, does attending church on Sundays make you more eager the more you attend, or does it make you less eager? Does coming to Belvedere feel good? "Yes." Do people who say it feels good doze off like this?

Recently, I have been thinking of moving all the members around here in Belvedere and New York to San Francisco or Los Angeles and bringing people from those areas here. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Why do I think like that? It is necessary. I can do it right away. Can I go? "Yes." Then they will say, "Oh, Belvedere..." (Laughter)

I saw that letter. They expressed it in a special way, but did they really like coming to Belvedere while they were in America? If they had that mindset and sang praises every day and worked hard every day, they wouldn’t have been sent away. If they were working just to say, "Oh, Teacher! When I go to Belvedere, I want to bring glory before heaven with a result..." why would they be sent away? Why? That’s how it is. People are just like that. People need training, people need hardship, and sometimes they need rebuke... that’s how it is. Does God like everything? Does God like this or that? "No." What does God like? Does God like those who cannot do it, or does God like those who can do it? "Those who can do it." Does God like the people who come in the morning and doze off, or does He like those who do not doze off? "Those who do not doze off." It’s the same. You should think that you need to teach this to thousands and tens of thousands of people using the Teacher’s words, and not just as they are, but that you will refine them more and teach them. In various ways, God likes those who strive harder and those who make more effort. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That is for sure. Isn’t it? "Yes."

From that perspective, among those who have been in here for three years or five years and think habitually, and those who have just joined and want to do something, which type do you think God would prefer? "The one who just joined..." Among those who are dozing off first in the front and those who are here for the first time this morning and say, "Oh, that’s Reverend Moon!" which one do you think God would focus on? "The one who just joined..." The dozing people are all cast aside.

What does that mean? You need to know that there are people who are stealing everything you have worked hard for until now. They are being transferred. Heaven takes by force. Those who doze off should not come forward as much as possible. They should sit in the back. What good does it do to rush here early to sit in the front and then doze off? If I come here and see that you are dozing off three times, I will remember you as "Oh, that woman who dozed off at any time..." and that would be a great misfortune. When it comes time to bless, I will remember, "Oh, you are the one who dozed off." (Laughter) That could happen.

It’s not just about dozing off. God is watching you 24 hours a day, so He is observing all your actions. When God sees, there are many people who are doing things even worse than dozing off. When you see people going somewhere, whether they are going to evangelize or do something else, God will compare the passion they show when they go with thousands and tens of thousands of people.

These kids… Can they take half a month to move? Such people should all resign in the future. I am not that kind of person. I did not do that. When I gave an order, I acted within three days. You all should not have that kind of mindset. If you do not come, close the door. Close the door and go where you need to go.

What problems have there been with personnel changes until now? People have been trying to take their own people with them. They have been thinking like that. What will the next person do? If you have that kind of mindset, your intentions will not be realized. Can someone going for the whole be thinking like that? Neil! If there is such a person in the future, report it and make personnel changes!

Did Dr. Bergman come? “Yes.” He said to me the other day that he would bring some people from Los Angeles… So I asked what he meant, and I said that it cannot be done. Can that be allowed? You should not have that kind of mindset. Your successor should do better than you. To do that, you must leave all your important people behind and be able to hand over to the new person, saying this person has this kind of talent and that kind of talent. 

That way, the foundation remains; if you take all the important people away, it will collapse entirely. It will collapse entirely. Those in charge here must eliminate such a mindset in the future. We must start eliminating it now.

Even at the training center, while working hard to train, I took all the important leaders and sent them all away. Then, oh, the leaders… What is education? The one who is educating is wrong. So, I sent all the important members away. A considerable number of state representatives all went out like that. What kind of mindset is that? If you have that kind of mindset… That is the thought of “Oh, the bigger my stage gets, the better people I should use so that I can be comfortable.” That cannot be. The bigger the stage gets, the more you should think about enduring hardships and nurturing people. That is how this organization develops.

When I came from Washington to New York, I moved all 80 people. I did not keep anyone with more skill than the local front line. So, I made all personnel changes. You all need to understand my mindset. We must strengthen the front line. The front line must be strong to handle everything; only then can the rear be solid. If the front line is weak and the rear is solid, what can we do? Then we are always subject to invasion. So, you all are in charge, and if the church youth under you are capable, quickly push them to the front line. You must nurture the less capable second string while working in the church.

Think about it. In 1975, even with intense repeated conferences in America ahead, we took the most important people and sent them out as missionaries, cutting off our waist, and to compensate for that, we trained new people and replaced them. Do you think that is easy? Do you know how much effort I put into that? That is why we must strengthen education. We must educate. We must strengthen the training center and provide education.

This year, I have tried to put all the important figures into the seminary as much as possible. Good people should be sent out repeatedly, and leaders must work hard to arrange and nurture new people. They must take full responsibility for teaching. Only then can we develop. It is a scientific conclusion that we cannot expect development without establishing such principled traditions. Therefore, when moving or doing anything, we must absolutely not take people with us. Do you understand? “Yes.”

Next, what about the leaders? They are all about money… Some guys are raising funds and taking the money with them. They leave behind debts. From now on, the American church must bear all costs.

Do you understand? That’s what you earn in a day. Even if you work every day, you can’t survive. So, you don’t know what kind of hardships your seniors faced behind the scenes. You don’t know.
