So, are you interested in ginseng tea? "Yes." After hearing this, you say "yes." It's the same in Japan. When they sell flowers, they are quick. When they go out to sell, they sell more than ginseng tea. Initially, the income is more than double. It keeps repeating, but ginseng tea, once opened, people will keep consuming it for their entire lives.

Then, how much do they promote it to the people around them, saying that ginseng tea is good? Once it starts to sell, the economic base... As time goes on, the number of salespeople decreases, but the quantity increases, and they can deliver it all... You can acquire vast capital from this.

Thus, because capital can be used in Japan, we have laid the foundation to help all of America. That's why we can bear the losses of $200,000 to $300,000 a month from newspapers and still have enough left over to engage in such activities. Now, the Unification Church in Japan can proudly declare that it is wealthy, that Reverend Moon has a lot of money, and that the Unification Church is rich.

This was earned over three years, over three years. In America, it won't even take three years because the market is wider. In two years, or even a year and a half, it will rise. 

At first, the Japanese members didn't want to do it at all. They thought the teacher was trying to make them suffer by creating a factory to sell Korean ginseng. They thought the teacher couldn't do it, just like everyone else, and there were all sorts of people. But these days, they say, "Oh, thank you, teacher." 

Look. How is selling peanuts different from selling ginseng tea? How is it different from setting up a store and delivering it? In that area, the upper class of the city becomes all customers. (Laughter) I was someone who didn't believe in ginseng. I thought a healthy person like me didn't need medicine or ginseng tea, and I scoffed at it, thinking it wouldn't be effective.

But when I made it myself, I tried it just to test it. You know ginseng candy, right? Just eating one in the morning means you can skip lunch without any problem. You won't feel the need for lunch... Do you understand what I mean? My hands, which used to be dry, started sweating when I began eating this. Also, in winter, I used to feel cold, but these days, I feel hot. I think that once someone going through menopause starts eating this, they will sell their house and their wife to buy it. (Laughter) Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

I told Bohee to eat a whole bottle because she said she had no strength in her legs, and how was it? "Yes, I started sweating..." So, think about it and talk about it. (Referring to President Park Bohee) It has a mysterious power, a mysterious power. There is no doubt about it. That's why if you take it regularly, you feel youthful, youthful. Wouldn't someone with money want to eat this? Once you start eating this, you won't need alcohol anymore.

Now, how wonderful a product this is. No matter how expensive it is, people love it and welcome it. Where else can you find such a business? Moreover, it works really well for Americans. Just think about how big this market is. I believe that once the American market is fully developed, it will exceed $30 million a month, $30 million. In a year, we can develop a market worth $400 million, in a year.

Now, that $400 million is the cost. Even if we sell it at five times the cost, that revenue will come into the American church. Will that money be spent all in America? What will you do with all that money? Will you buy Ford Motor Company or not? Will you buy the Empire State Building or not? "Yes." It will definitely happen.

So, is this worth doing or not? Can you all buy a building like East Garden or Belvedere? Will you do it or not? "We will." Once you realize that, everyone, even the association president, will quit their position and want to do this business. "Let me be the president!" They will say. (Laughter) That can happen.

Engage in three-dimensional sales activities.

To do such business, everything I mentioned earlier is connected. Everything I said earlier is connected, in a three-dimensional way... By working on one thing, you can do three or four businesses; that's what smart people do. Why wouldn't you do this? Do you feel like doing it? "Yes." Now you can believe it. If you don't believe it, call Germany, call Japan, and see if it's true or not. Call Switzerland, call Martin Porter, and ask if it's true or not.

So, do you need money? "Yes." Once you sell it, will you sell things that don't sell more and more, or will you sell things that people keep coming back to buy? Which one will you choose? If you go out with a bouquet of flowers, will you sell peanuts while driving a truck, or will you stack things on a van and deliver them? Which one will you choose? "In the truck..." How wonderful, and how dignified is the authority of the business? And people who eat it, no matter how expensive it is, will come back and say thank you, not "This guy tricked me."

Now, starting this year, the best products recognized by the Korean government are rated with four stars. (Writing while speaking) This is the best. Then there are two stars, and they all have these markings. That's why people will immediately know that our products are the best.

Think about it. The principle is that ginseng tea should contain more than 15% ginseng, but we put in 29%. Do you understand? Why did we do that? To ensure the medicinal effect. Since we put in more than double, it can't be compared. Is there anyone who sells like that? That's why this is the first in the world. Even if ginseng from the communist world comes out, they will all try to suppress it. They are doing that now. Do you understand? That's why the government thinks our product is a little better than the ordinary ones. The government thinks our product is slightly better. They don't know everything; we are strategically moving forward. Once they eat it for a year, everyone will know immediately.

They don't know whether ginseng tea contains 15% or 7% ginseng. The general public doesn't know. Even if it's 7%, it doesn't matter. They don't know. That's why, in the global market, the government is now creating this system to recognize high-quality Korean products. Do you understand? So think of it as the best ginseng tea in the world. This is no doubt.

How does this happen? Why does it happen? We have researched the machinery to extract ginseng extract, and we can produce more than double what a regular factory can produce. The ginseng factory is the only one of its kind in the world. Do you understand what I mean?

Now, let's see who wants to sell ginseng tea. Think about the two years of hard work. After that, it will definitely rise. There is no doubt about it. And in America, since document sales are needed, if we just advertise nationwide, it can sell a lot. If we just advertise, it can sell nationwide.

Looking at the current situation in Korea, next year, even if we sell a lot of ginseng in America...
There are no items to bring. Exporting to Japan has become a problem right now because there are no raw materials. So, I instructed to invest 15 million dollars this year to buy land and purchase more ginseng that is two or three years old. So, how are you thinking about preparing for sales in the U.S. in the future? We have to do that, right? "Yes." We need to make it so that people can consume it as easily as eating rice. If we prepare everything like coffee, that would be incredible. How great would that be? (laughs) If that happens, even if we serve coffee-like products to guests, they won't want to eat them. That's bad for the body, so why would they eat it?

Now, you understand without further explanation, right? You understand now? "Yes." So, do you want to sell it? "Yes." Do you want to sell it, George Hurlensler? "Yes." (laughs) If you manage to sell it even with difficulty, all the problems will be solved. Right now, the inventory of ginseng tea... Look. I haven't touched it because I can't until after the Washington conference and the Yankee Stadium event, but starting next year, I will get involved. Do you understand?

So, do you all want to do it? "Yes." You can do evangelism and sell ginseng tea... But that's not possible. You can't do it if you want to eat it. The economic issues of that week will be resolved depending on who among you lays the foundation steadily first. This will sequentially create a formal difference. So, not only ginseng tea but also ginseng extract will be made into capsules, and I've prepared everything so that Americans will need it.

Let's talk about ginseng extract. Ginseng extract is imported from Japan, and since it is an agricultural processed product, there are no taxes. There are no taxes. However, ginseng tea incurs a 25% import tax. So, this year, the message is to sell ginseng extract. In Japan, they campaigned to sell this for $180 per 300 grams.

As it started selling in bulk, the Japanese government questioned whether it was fake... (writing on the board) Genuine products are going out like this, but they can make something that looks and tastes the same for just $18. How can they believe that? So, the Japanese government specially commissioned a thorough analysis and research on how expensive this is. They concluded that it cannot be this expensive. They planned to take down the Unification Church with this. Several pharmacists analyzed it and found it to be very good. They concluded that it should be worth $120. Do you understand what that means? So, they went "shh— shh—." Our information department found all this out. The government was quiet, but once they find out, how much do you think they will sell? (laughs) Do you understand?

So, this is undeniable. This is among medicinal materials... Even if Japanese people try to make it as medicine, they can't. After switching from ginseng tea to ginseng extract, sales nearly doubled. Do you understand? So, the U.S. should sell ginseng tea now, but in the future, we must urgently push for extract sales. It is now the Christmas season, which is a sale period. This will continue through December and January. We have about $500,000 worth of inventory, and we need to sell it all. Do you want to sell it? "Yes."

When we import it, it costs more than $5 per 200 grams. Since it has been over a year and a half since it came in, with interest, it costs about $7. It exceeds $6. This is not something to discuss with outsiders. Even if you know today, keep it quiet. You shouldn't talk about it when selling. Now, how much are we going to sell it for? We are selling it for $25.

So, how much do we pass it on for...? (writing while speaking) There are 100-gram and 200-gram packages, and if we pass it to the department store for $15, they will sell it for $25. If we pass the 200-gram package to the department store for $15, how much will we pass the 100-gram package for? If it's $7.50, then combining the 100-gram and 200-gram packages, it totals $22.50. Do you understand what I mean?

Kamiya, how much is the cost for 100 grams? It is sold for $13, but the cost is $4, right? "The cost is $3.05." Didn't you say it was $4? "For 100 grams, it's $3.05." $3.05? "Yes." Then, adding the $7 for the 200-gram package, it totals $10.50, and we will give it to you for $10. In the next two months, we will pass it on at cost. We are planning to pass the 300-gram package at cost. Now, how many do we have? There are 45,000 of the 200-gram packages and 30,000 of the 100-gram packages. Do you understand what I mean? Kamiya, do we have a lot? "Yes." You need to sell all of that within these two months. "Yes, I will do that."

So, we are trying to import extract in capsules. Selling is the same. Generally, it's $25 and the 100-gram package is... how much did you say? "It's $13." $13? We will continue to sell it, so we will set that as a principle, but then quietly go and not tell anyone and do it specially... You are to do it appropriately. Even in general department stores, this is $15, and these two packages for $22.50 will go for more. So, you shouldn't sell it for less than that. You need to know that. However, if someone buys a 200-gram package for $25, it is okay to give them a 100-gram package for free. Giving it away... So, selling it for $25 is certain. One is a gift. If the department store finds out, it will be a big problem. Do you understand? "Yes."

Kamiya! What are you going to do? From this month, there are 18 locations... There are 18 locations across all states in the U.S., so come by car and sell it. Keep doing it. Instead, you need to write a check and go, in cash. Why? Because we need to order from Korea immediately, and it takes more than three months to get the order. Only then will the items you can sell come.

So, if you sell one, you can buy it back for double, so you can increase it as much as you want. Three times seven is twenty-one (3×7=21), so you can buy more than three times, which means you can develop it without having a lot of money. So, when you go this time, report to Kamiya how much you think you can sell in two months. That way, we can prepare and arrange everything here. You will have to take responsibility for that. Do you understand? Kamiya! "Yes." Prepare for that. "Yes, I understand." Whatever it takes, make sure to sell everything within these two months. "Yes."

Then there is the deadline issue, but if the deadline passes, it takes six months to import by ship. That should be fine. That won't be a problem. Now, do you all understand? It's already six-thirty.

We need to create a traditional form through worship and prayer life. I have mostly shared my instructions today. What I talked about today is mostly instructions. Do you understand? You should have a rough idea of what to do this year. From next year, we will focus on this. So, we need to prepare everything so that we can all practice this as we know it.

Now, if we import ginseng tea worth a million dollars each month next year, we will have an income of five million dollars a month. If we do this for a year, it will triple. We will have three times the profit in a year. Why? Because one person will definitely promote it to three people. Then next, it will exceed three million dollars. Once it exceeds three million dollars, it will then rise to ten million dollars. Then it will rise to thirty million dollars. If we start with a million dollars next year, it will reach that standard within four years. It is not a distant story. Do you understand? Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." There are miraculous economic resources here, miraculous. So, if you have the will, give it a try. This is certain. So, keep that in mind...

Time has passed a lot; how long will it take to get to Radio City in New York? "It will take about an hour and a half from here." What time does it end? Around nine o'clock? These days, there is a Christmas show, so it would be nice to go and see it. Let's have dinner and go quickly... Do you want to see that? (applause) How many people are there? "There are 115 people." Then how much is that in total, since it's $400 each? Let's have dinner here...

And one more thing to mention? I plan to go to Las Vegas on the 8th, where Elvis Presley is currently performing. I want to take Elvis Presley to Tokyo to sign a show contract, so I plan to go and listen to him. I need to pick twelve people to go with me; I would like to bring two from the West and ten from our guards here. From the West, I will call Dr. Dust and Neil.

And during Christmas, I told the seminary students to send anyone who can go. They can invite people from their homes or special cases, but if everyone from the MFT activities goes, it will be a big problem, so it would be good if they could bring their parents to meet during that week. If their parents send travel expenses and problems arise, they can send them if possible, but it will be difficult to move this time. If you see that a parent is sending travel expenses and it becomes a problem, you should send them, but do not force it.

And everyone, we have our meals on Sundays and the first morning of the month. And if possible, we should gather on Wednesdays and Sunday evenings... Seven o'clock in the evening would be good. Until now, we couldn't keep it because of events like the Yankee Stadium conference, but that can't continue. If we do not hold formal worship in the future, we will receive many accusations from established churches. Established churches think we do not hold worship or read the Bible. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, until now, we had no choice but to do that, but starting next year, we need to formally revive this and create an atmosphere where we can evangelize relatives and friends at this time. Then, we need to create a traditional form that does not fall behind established churches regarding hymn leading, prayer, and preaching.

And the circuit members should diligently travel around, and if there are special matters, tell Sang-cheol. He used to do well but hasn't been doing it lately. Contact Mrs. Choi (Choi Won-bok). If there are special matters, it would be good to have Mrs. Choi report to the teacher. Do you understand? (President Park Bo-hee prays)

Tomorrow morning, we will start at six, so if you want to attend, you can, and if you don't, that's fine. You can leave if you want. Tomorrow morning, there will be a gathering here.

And Neil... When you all go back, what you need to do is that the first day of the next year is God's Day, and it is the day that marks the beginning of 300 years for America, so it is a historical day from our perspective, and we need to celebrate it well.

So, you need to plan ahead for the principle lecture conference, singing competition, and everything. You need to plan for all the competitions. Start planning from now. You should prepare to participate in these competitions when you come back home.

You will probably need to attend here on the morning of the 31st for all the meetings. In the afternoon, those who can attend together... We will have those meetings and everything at that time. So, you need to come on the 31st and prepare everything. Everyone should be here by ten o'clock. I am thinking of holding all the meetings before that. And Bo-hee, we need to hurry up with the preparations for the broadcast we were planning. *
